<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Uses native CSS Scroll Snap</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports horizontal and vertical orientations</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports slide alignment (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">start</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">center</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">end</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports showing multiple slides at a time</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports looping and auto-playing</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports custom spacing between slides</li>
</ul>

<p>Check the carousel anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the carousel package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> carousel</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/carousel&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The carousel package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Note:</strong> The carousel requires that you provide a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slideCount</code> property in
the machine context. This is the total number of slides.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">vertical</code> to render a vertical carousel.</p>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-slide" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial slide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-slide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPage</code> corresponds to the scroll snap position index based on the
layout. It does not necessarily correspond to the index of the slide in the
carousel.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="setting-slides-per-page" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting slides per page<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-slides-per-page"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerPage</code> to control how many slides are visible per page.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">slidesPerPage</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-slides-per-move" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting slides per move<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-slides-per-move"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerMove</code> to control how many slides advance on next/previous.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">slidesPerMove</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Considerations</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">If the value is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">auto</code>, the carousel will move the number of slides equal to
the number of slides per page.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Ensure the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerMove</code> is less than or equal to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerPage</code> to
avoid skipping slides.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">On touch devices, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerMove</code> is not enforced during active swiping. The
browser&#x27;s native scrolling and CSS Scroll Snap determine slide movement for
optimal performance and UX.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="looping-pages" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Looping pages<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#looping-pages"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loop</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to wrap around from last to first page.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="listening-for-page-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for page changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-page-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the carousel page changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { page: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;selected page:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">page</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h3 id="listening-for-drag-and-autoplay-status" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for drag and autoplay status<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-drag-and-autoplay-status"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use status callbacks to react to dragging and autoplay lifecycle changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onAutoplayStatusChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">type</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">isPlaying</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="dragging-the-carousel" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Dragging the carousel<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#dragging-the-carousel"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowMouseDrag</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to drag the carousel with a mouse.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowMouseDrag</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="autoplaying-the-carousel" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Autoplaying the carousel<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#autoplaying-the-carousel"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoplay</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to start automatic slide movement.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoplay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Alternatively, you can configure the autoplay interval by setting the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">delay</code>
property.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoplay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">delay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2000</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-messages" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility messages<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-messages"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize localized trigger, item, and progress text.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>carousel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">slideCount</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">nextTrigger</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Next slide&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">prevTrigger</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Previous slide&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">indicator</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">index</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Go to slide </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>index <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">item</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> count</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Slide </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>index <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> of </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>count<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">autoplayStart</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Start autoplay&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">autoplayStop</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Stop autoplay&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">progressText</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> page<span class="token punctuation">,</span> totalPages <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Page </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>page <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> of </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>totalPages<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the root part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-group&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item-group part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the root part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the control part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;next-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the next-trigger part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;prev-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the prev-trigger part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator-group&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the indicator-group part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the indicator part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;autoplay-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the autoplay-trigger part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="active-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Active state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#active-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a carousel&#x27;s indicator is active, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-current</code> attribute is set on the
indicator.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-current</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the indicator&#x27;s active state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The carousel&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods and properties:</p>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The carousel machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; item: (index: number) =&gt; string; itemGroup: string; nextTrigger: string; prevTrigger: string; indicatorGroup: string; indicator: (index: number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the carousel. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">The localized messages to use.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The number of slides to show at a time.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to enable variable width slides.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slidesPerMove</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number | &quot;auto&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The number of slides to scroll at a time.

When set to `auto`, the number of slides to scroll is determined by the
`slidesPerPage` property.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoplay</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean | { delay: number; }</code><span class="d_block">Whether to scroll automatically. The default delay is 4000ms.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowMouseDrag</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow scrolling via dragging with mouse</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loop</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the carousel should loop around.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">page</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled page of the carousel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial page to scroll to when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the page of the carousel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">spacing</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The amount of space between items.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">padding</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">Defines the extra space added around the scrollable area,
enabling nearby items to remain partially in view.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PageChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the page changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inViewThreshold</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number | number[]</code><span class="d_block">The threshold for determining if an item is in view.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">snapType</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;proximity&quot; | &quot;mandatory&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The snap type of the item.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slideCount</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of slides.
Useful for SSR to render the initial ating the snap points.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onDragStatusChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: DragStatusDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the drag status changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onAutoplayStatusChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: AutoplayStatusDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the autoplay status changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the element.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The carousel <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">page</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The current index of the carousel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pageSnapPoints</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The current snap points of the carousel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isPlaying</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the carousel is auto playing</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isDragging</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the carousel is being dragged. This only works when `draggable` is true.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">canScrollNext</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the carousel is can scroll to the next view</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">canScrollPrev</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the carousel is can scroll to the previous view</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToIndex</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number, instant?: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to scroll to a specific item index</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollTo</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(page: number, instant?: boolean) =&gt; and clamp the page</span></li></ul>

\u003ccode\u003epage\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonPageChange\u003c/code\u003e for controlled navigation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slideCount: 8,\n  page,\n  onPageChange(details) {\n    setPage(details.page)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting slides per page\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eslidesPerPage\u003c/code\u003e to control how many slides are visible per page.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slidesPerMove: 2,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConsiderations\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf the value is \u003ccode\u003eauto\u003c/code\u003e, the carousel will move the number of slides equal to\nthe number of slides per page.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnsure the \u003ccode\u003eslidesPerMove\u003c/code\u003e is less than or equal to the \u003ccode\u003eslidesPerPage\u003c/code\u003e to\navoid skipping slides.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOn touch devices, \u003ccode\u003eslidesPerMove\u003c/code\u003e is not enforced during active swiping. Snap for smooth,\nperformant scrolling between slides.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/carousel\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Carousel\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Uses native CSS Scroll Snap\n- Supports horizontal and vertical orientations\n- Supports slide alignment (`start`, `center`, `end`)\n- Supports showing multiple slides at a time\n- Supports looping and auto-playing\n- Supports custom spacing between slides\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the carousel package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"carousel/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the carousel anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"carousel\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the carousel package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as carousel from \"@zag-js/carousel\"\n```\n\nThe carousel package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003e **Note:** The carousel requires that you provide a `slideCount` property in\n\u003e the machine context. This is the total number of slides.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"carousel/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Vertical orientation\n\nSet `orientation` to `vertical` to render a vertical carousel.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the initial slide\n\nSet `defaultPage` to define the initial page.\n\n\u003e The `defaultPage` corresponds to the scroll snap position index based on the\n\u003e layout. It does not necessarily correspond to the index of the slide in the\n\u003e carousel.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  defaultPage: 2,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling the current page\n\nUse `page` and `onPageChange` for controlled navigation.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slideCount: 8,\n  page,\n  onPageChange(details) {\n    setPage(details.page)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Setting slides per page\n\nSet `slidesPerPage` to control how many slides are visible per page.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slidesPerPage: 2,\n})\n```\n\n### Setting slides per move\n\nSet `slidesPerMove` to control how many slides advance on next/previous.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slidesPerMove: 2,\n})\n```\n\n**Considerations**\n\n- If the value is `auto`, the carousel will move the number of slides equal to\n  the number of slides per page.\n- Ensure the `slidesPerMove` is less than or equal to the `slidesPerPage` to\n  avoid skipping slides.\n- On touch devices, `slidesPerMove` is not enforced during active swiping. The\n  browser's native scrolling and CSS Scroll Snap determine slide movement for\n  optimal performance and UX.\n\n### Looping pages\n\nSet `loop` to `true` to wrap around from last to first page.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  loop: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the gap between slides\n\nSet `spacing` to control the gap between slides.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  spacing: \"16px\",\n})\n```\n\n### Setting viewport padding\n\nSet `padding` to keep neighboring slides partially visible.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  padding: \"16px\",\n})\n```\n\n### Variable-width slides\n\nSet `autoSize` to `true` when slides have different widths.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  autoSize: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for page changes\n\nWhen the carousel page changes, the `onPageChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  onPageChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { page: number }\n    console.log(\"selected page:\", details.page)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for drag and autoplay status\n\nUse status callbacks to react to dragging and autoplay lifecycle changes.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  onDragStatusChange(details) {\n    console.log(details.type, details.isDragging)\n  },\n  onAutoplayStatusChange(details) {\n    console.log(details.type, details.isPlaying)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Dragging the carousel\n\nSet `allowMouseDrag` to `true` to drag the carousel with a mouse.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  allowMouseDrag: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Autoplaying the carousel\n\nSet `autoplay` to `true` to start automatic slide movement.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  autoplay: true,\n})\n```\n\nAlternatively, you can configure the autoplay interval by setting the `delay`\nproperty.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  autoplay: { delay: 2000 },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility messages\n\nUse `translations` to customize localized trigger, item, and progress text.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(carousel.machine, {\n  slideCount: 5,\n  translations: {\n    nextTrigger: \"Next slide\",\n    prevTrigger: \"Previous slide\",\n    indicator: (index) =\u003e `Go to slide ${index + 1}`,\n    item: (index, count) =\u003e `Slide ${index + 1} of ${count}`,\n    autoplayStart: \"Start autoplay\",\n    autoplayStop: \"Stop autoplay\",\n    progressText: ({ page, totalPages }) =\u003e `Page ${page + 1} of ${totalPages}`,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item-group\"] {\n  /* styles for the item-group part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"] {\n  /* styles for the control part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"next-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the next-trigger part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"prev-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the prev-trigger part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"indicator-group\"] {\n  /* styles for the indicator-group part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"indicator\"] {\n  /* styles for the indicator part */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"autoplay-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the autoplay-trigger part */\n}\n```\n\n### Active state\n\nWhen a carousel's indicator is active, a `data-current` attribute is set on the\nindicator.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"indicator\"][data-current] {\n  /* styles for the indicator's active state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\nThe carousel's `api` exposes the following methods and properties:\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe carousel machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"carousel\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe carousel `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"carousel\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"carousel\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"carousel\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Carousel\",\"description\":\"Using the carousel machine in your
